<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people_from_Bogot.C3.A1">Notable people from Bogotá</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Notable people from Bogotá">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arturo_Acevedo_Vallarino" title="Arturo Acevedo Vallarino">Arturo Acevedo Vallarino</a> (1873-1950), director of silent films</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Haider_Ackermann" title="Haider Ackermann">Haider Ackermann</a> (1971–), fashion designer</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_%C3%81lvarez_(writer)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sergio Álvarez (writer) (page does not exist)">Sergio Álvarez</a> (born 1965), writer and journalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alberto_Castilla" title="Alberto Castilla">Alberto Castilla</a> (1883–1938), engineer, journalist, poet, writer, mathematician and musician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Guillermo_Cano_Isaza" title="Guillermo Cano Isaza">Guillermo Cano Isaza</a> (1925-1986), journalist and editor of the <a href="/wiki/El_Espectador" title="El Espectador">El Espectador</a> newspaper</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miguel_Antonio_Caro" title="Miguel Antonio Caro">Miguel Antonio Caro</a> (1843-1909), politician and 1894-1898 President of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Cepeda_Ulloa" title="Fernando Cepeda Ulloa">Fernando Cepeda Ulloa</a> (1938–), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Vicente_Concha" title="José Vicente Concha">José Vicente Concha</a> (1867-1929), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Esteban_Cort%C3%A1zar" title="Esteban Cortázar">Esteban Cortázar</a> (1984–), fashion designer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rufino_Jos%C3%A9_Cuervo" title="Rufino José Cuervo">Rufino José Cuervo</a> (1844–1911), writer, linguist and philologist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Domingo_Duquesne" title="José Domingo Duquesne">José Domingo Duquesne</a> (1748-1822), theologist and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Muisca_scholars" title="List of Muisca scholars">Muisca scholar</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hernando_Dur%C3%A1n_Duss%C3%A1n" title="Hernando Durán Dussán">Hernando Durán Dussán</a> (1920-1998), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andrea_Echeverri" title="Andrea Echeverri">Andrea Echeverri</a> (1965–), musician, lead singer of <a href="/wiki/Aterciopelados" title="Aterciopelados">Aterciopelados</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Santiago_Gamboa" title="Santiago Gamboa">Santiago Gamboa</a> (1965–), writer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rodrigo_Garc%C3%ADa_(director)" title="Rodrigo García (director)">Rodrigo García</a> (1959–), film director, son of <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Garc%C3%ADa_M%C3%A1rquez" title="Gabriel García Márquez">Gabriel García Márquez</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_G%C3%B3mez_Hurtado" title="Álvaro Gómez Hurtado">Álvaro Gómez Hurtado</a> (1919–1995), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Laureano_G%C3%B3mez" title="Laureano Gómez">Laureano Gómez</a> (1889-1965), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miguel_G%C3%B3mez_(photographer)" title="Miguel Gómez (photographer)">Miguel Gómez</a> (1974–), photographer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ana_Mar%C3%ADa_Groot" title="Ana María Groot">Ana María Groot</a> (1952-), anthropologist and archaeologist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_B._Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Juan B. Gutiérrez">Juan B. Gutiérrez</a>, (1973-), writer and mathematician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rudolf_Hommes_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Rudolf Hommes Rodríguez">Rudolf Hommes Rodríguez</a> (1943–), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Leguizamo" title="John Leguizamo">John Leguizamo</a> (1964–), actor and comedian</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alfonso_L%C3%B3pez_Caballero" title="Alfonso López Caballero">Alfonso López Caballero</a> (1944–), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alberto_Lleras_Camargo" title="Alberto Lleras Camargo">Alberto Lleras Camargo</a> (1906–1990), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlos_Lleras_Restrepo" title="Carlos Lleras Restrepo">Carlos Lleras Restrepo</a> (1908–1994), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rodolfo_Llin%C3%A1s" title="Rodolfo Llinás">Rodolfo Llinás</a> (1934–), neuroscientist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Novoa" title="Rafael Novoa">Rafael Novoa</a> (1971–), actor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chucho_Merch%C3%A1n" title="Chucho Merchán">Chucho Merchán</a> (1952–), bassist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Antanas_Mockus" title="Antanas Mockus">Antanas Mockus</a> (1952–), politician, philosopher, mathematician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Pablo_Montoya" title="Juan Pablo Montoya">Juan Pablo Montoya</a> (1975–), race car driver</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ana_Mar%C3%ADa_Orozco" title="Ana María Orozco">Ana María Orozco</a> (1973–), actress</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Pardo_Rueda" title="Rafael Pardo Rueda">Rafael Pardo Rueda</a> (1953–), politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joaqu%C3%ADn_Par%C3%ADs_Ricaurte" title="Joaquín París Ricaurte">Joaquín París Ricaurte</a> (1795-1898), independence hero</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Pastrana_Arango" title="Andrés Pastrana Arango">Andrés Pastrana Arango</a> (1954–), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Enrique_Pe%C3%B1alosa" title="Enrique Peñalosa">Enrique Peñalosa</a> (1955–), mayor of Bogotá (2016-2019), urbanist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Pablo_Plata_Figueroa" title="Juan Pablo Plata Figueroa">Juan Pablo Plata Figueroa</a>, (1982-), writer and journalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Pombo" title="Rafael Pombo">Rafael Pombo</a> (1833–1912), poet, writer and diplomat</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Puyana" title="Rafael Puyana">Rafael Puyana</a> (1931–2013), harpsichordist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Robles_(cyclist)" title="José Robles (cyclist)">José Robles</a> (1964-), former professional cyclist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Clara_Rojas" title="Clara Rojas">Clara Rojas</a> (born 1964), politician, lawyer and former FARC hostage</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Daniel_Samper_Pizano" title="Daniel Samper Pizano">Daniel Samper Pizano</a> (1945–), journalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ernesto_Samper" title="Ernesto Samper">Ernesto Samper</a> (1950–), former president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Patricio_Samper_Gnecco" title="Patricio Samper Gnecco">Patricio Samper Gnecco</a> (1930–2006), architect, politician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Catalina_Sandino_Moreno" title="Catalina Sandino Moreno">Catalina Sandino Moreno</a> (1981–), actress</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Manuel_Santos" title="Juan Manuel Santos">Juan Manuel Santos</a> (1951–), current president of Colombia</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eugene_Semple" title="Eugene Semple">Eugene Semple</a> (1840-1908), American politician and from 1887 to 1889 the 13th Governor of <a href="/wiki/Washington_Territory" title="Washington Territory">Washington Territory</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Asunci%C3%B3n_Silva" title="José Asunción Silva">José Asunción Silva</a> (1865–1896), poet, writer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miguel_Triana" title="Miguel Triana">Miguel Triana</a> (1859-1931), engineer and Muisca scholar</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Diana_Turbay" title="Diana Turbay">Diana Turbay</a> (1950–1991), journalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Liborio_Zerda" title="Liborio Zerda">Liborio Zerda</a> (1834-1919), physician and Muisca scholar</li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bibliography_and_further_reading_on_pre-Columbian_Bogot.C3.A1">Bibliography and further reading on pre-Columbian Bogotá</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Bibliography and further reading on pre-Columbian Bogotá">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pre-Muisca">Pre-Muisca</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Pre-Muisca">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BGonzalo_Correal_Urrego.7CCorreal_Urrego.5D.5D1990"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Correal_Urrego" title="Gonzalo Correal Urrego">Correal Urrego</a>, Gonzalo</span>. 1990. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://peru.inka.free.fr/Runapacha/pleiscol.pdf">Evidencias culturales durante el Pleistocene y Holoceno de Colombia - Cultural evidences during the Pleistocene and Holocene of Colombia</a>. <i>Revista de Arqueología Americana</i> 1. 69–89. Accessed 2016-07-08.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy_2">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BList_of_Muisca_research_institutes.7CArg.C3.BCello_Garc.C3.ADa.5D.5D2015"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/List_of_Muisca_research_institutes" title="List of Muisca research institutes">Argüello García</a>, Pedro María</span>. 2015. <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://d-scholarship.pitt.edu/24491/1/Arguello_P._Subsistence_economy.pdf">Subsistence economy and chiefdom emergence in the Muisca area. A study of the Valle de Tena (PhD)</a></i>, 1–193. <a href="/wiki/University_of_Pittsburgh" title="University of Pittsburgh">University of Pittsburgh</a>. Accessed 2016-07-08.</li>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BList_of_Muisca_research_institutes.7CFrancis.5D.5D1993"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/List_of_Muisca_research_institutes" title="List of Muisca research institutes">Francis</a>, John Michael</span>. 1993. <i>"Muchas hipas, no minas" The Muiscas, a merchant society: Spanish misconceptions and demographic change (M.A.)</i>, 1-118. <a href="/wiki/University_of_Alberta" title="University of Alberta">University of Alberta</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Society_.26_tunjos">Society &amp; <i><a href="/wiki/Tunjo" title="Tunjo">tunjos</a></i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Society &amp; tunjos">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BJago_Cooper.7CCooper.5D.5D2013"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/Jago_Cooper" title="Jago Cooper">Cooper</a>, Jago</span>, and <span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Carl Henrik <a href="/wiki/Carl_Henrik_Langebaek" title="Carl Henrik Langebaek">Langebaek</a></span>. 2013. <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_sovvzUAVoA">The Lost Kingdoms of South America - Episode 3 - Lands of Gold</a></i>. Accessed 2016-07-14.</li>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BJorge_Gamboa_Mendoza.7CGamboa_Mendoza.5D.5D2016"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/Jorge_Gamboa_Mendoza" title="Jorge Gamboa Mendoza">Gamboa Mendoza</a>, Jorge</span>. 2016. <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NAJ-EM5h4N0">Los muiscas, grupos indígenas del Nuevo Reino de Granada. Una nueva propuesta sobre su organizacíon socio-política y su evolucíon en el siglo XVI - The Muisca, indigenous groups of the New Kingdom of Granada. A new proposal on their social-political organization and their evolution in the 16th century</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Gold_Museum,_Bogot%C3%A1" title="Gold Museum, Bogotá">Museo del Oro</a>. Accessed 2016-07-08.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Agriculture">Agriculture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Agriculture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BList_of_Muisca_research_institutes.7CBoada_Rivas.5D.5D2006"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/List_of_Muisca_research_institutes" title="List of Muisca research institutes">Boada Rivas</a>, Ana María</span>. 2006. <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pitt.edu/~ccapubs/books/br079.html">Patrones de asentamiento regional y sistemas de agricultura intensiva en Cota y Suba, Sabana de Bogotá (Colombia) - Regional settlement patterns and intensive agricultural systems in Cota and Suba, Bogotá savanna (Colombia)</a></i>, 1–181. <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_Republic_(Colombia)" title="Bank of the Republic (Colombia)">Banco de la República</a>. Accessed 2016-07-08.</li>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BSylvia_M._Broadbent.7CBroadbent.5D.5D1968"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/Sylvia_M._Broadbent" title="Sylvia M. Broadbent">Broadbent</a>, Sylvia M</span>. 1968. A prehistoric field system in Chibcha territory, Colombia. <i>Ñawpa Pacha: Journal of Andean Archaeology</i> 6. 135-147.</li>
</ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine_2">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bogot%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span id="CITEREF.5B.5BList_of_Muisca_research_institutes.7CDaza.5D.5D2013"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href="/wiki/List_of_Muisca_research_institutes" title="List of Muisca research institutes">Daza</a>, Blanca Ysabel</span>. 2013. <i>Historia del proceso de mestizaje alimentario entre Colombia y España - History of the integration process of foods between Colombia and Spain (PhD)</i>, 1-494. <a href="/wiki/Universitat_de_Barcelona" class="mw-redirect" title="Universitat de Barcelona">Universitat de Barcelona</a>.</li>
<li><span id="CITEREFDelgado_Burbano2014"></span><span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Delgado Burbano, Miguel</span>; <span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Carl Henrik Langebaek Rueda</span>; <span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Lucero Aristizábal</span>; <span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Robert Tykot</span>, and <span class="smallcaps" style="font-variant:small-caps;">Lauren Johnson</span>. 2014. Indicadores Bioquímicos de Dieta en Tibanica, un Poblado Muisca Tardío en la Sabana de Bogotá (Colombia): Isótopos Estables (δ13Ccol, δ13Cap y δ15N) y Elementos Traza (Ba y Sr) - Biochemical indicators of diet in Tibanica, a Late Muisca settlement on the Bogotá savanna (Colombia): Stable isotopes (δ13Ccol, δ13Cap and δ15N) and trace elements (Ba and Sr). <i>Avances Recientes de la Bioarqueología Latinoamericana</i> _. 103-127.</li>
</ul>
